I really do not get the comments saying this was a "mess." Besides the mic and slight wardrobe issues (which obviously weren't Twice's fault), I thought this was a fantastic performance. The live vocals were sweet, strong, and lovely to listen to. They had pretty good facial expressions for the most part (although I still would have liked to see more variety in their expressions). If you pause at any given moment, they are all in sync. This choreography has many moving parts and formations, and there are many times when members have their own individual movements. However, that doesn't mean this dance or performance is a mess - I think they executed the choreography wonderfully. I also thought their energy level was very appropriate for the concept of this song. It's a sensual song about the night after all.

Since some Onces continue to make fools of themselves in the comments... 1. Billboard does not own Youtube Theater, nor do run their own AV crew. The AV crew, the video streaming company, etc., all those are either hired by Billboard through an event manager, or are part of the services from Youtube theater. 2. Billboard is a client, who paid professionals to do the technical work. They are in the music business, not the mic business, nor the video streaming business. So I don't understand you kids who say that Billboard did Twice dirty (it wasn't their staff directly handling the mics), or that they should be more careful (again, not their staff). But y'all are so desperate to blame someone that it doesn't matter who, I guess. 3. If you want to complain, send a letter to either Billboard or Youtube theater and ask them the name of the companies who did the video streaming and the AV for the show, and tell them you want to be Blinks and go on a hate campaign.
